consumer group coordinator implements a state machine for managing group membership and rebalancing. The implementation is split between Classic groups (traditional protocol) and Modern groups (consumer protocol, share protocol, and streams protocol).\\n\\n**Classic Group State Machine:**\\nThe core state machine is defined in `ClassicGroupState.java` (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/classic/) with five states:\\n1. EMPTY - Group has no members, waiting for new members to join\\n2. PREPARING_REBALANCE - Group is in the join phase, collecting join requests from members\\n3. COMPLETING_REBALANCE - Group is in the sync phase, awaiting assignments from the leader\\n4. STABLE - All members have joined and synced, group is operational\\n5. DEAD - Group metadata is being removed\\n\\nThe valid state transitions are enforced through the `validPreviousStates` set in `ClassicGroupState`, defining the valid transitions:\\n- EMPTY → PREPARING_REBALANCE\\n- PREPARING_REBALANCE → COMPLETING_REBALANCE or EMPTY\\n- COMPLETING_REBALANCE → STABLE\\n- STABLE/PREPARING_REBALANCE/COMPLETING_REBALANCE/EMPTY → DEAD\\n\\n**Join Phase Implementation:**\\nMember join state is tracked in `ClassicGroupMember.java` with methods `isAwaitingJoin()` which checks if `awaitingJoinFuture` is set. When members send join requests, the `classicGroupJoin()` method in `GroupMetadataManager.java` processes them and manages the group's transition to PREPARING_REBALANCE. The flow calls `addMemberThenRebalanceOrCompleteJoin()` and `maybePrepareRebalanceOrCompleteJoin()` to coordinate the state transitions.\\n\\n**Sync Phase Implementation:**\\nMember sync state is tracked with `isAwaitingSync()` checking if `awaitingSyncFuture` is set. The `classicGroupSync()` method in `GroupMetadataManager.java` handles sync requests from members. Once all members have synced with their assignments, the group transitions from COMPLETING_REBALANCE to STABLE.\\n\\n**State Transitions:**\\nState transitions are managed through the `transitionTo()` method in `ClassicGroup.java`, which enforces valid transitions and tracks both current and previous states. Invalid transitions throw an `IllegalStateException`.\\n\\n**Modern Groups:**\\nModern consumer groups (`ConsumerGroup.java` in modern/consumer/) implement their own state machine with states: EMPTY, ASSIGNING, RECONCILING, STABLE, DEAD. consumer group coordinator implements a state machine for managing group membership and rebalancing. The implementation is split between Classic groups (traditional protocol) and Modern groups (consumer protocol, share protocol, and streams protocol).\\n\\n**Classic Group State Machine:**\\nThe core state machine is defined in `ClassicGroupState.java` (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/classic/) with five states:\\n1. EMPTY - Group has no members, waiting for new members to join\\n2. PREPARING_REBALANCE - Group is in the join phase, collecting join requests from members\\n3. COMPLETING_REBALANCE - Group is in the sync phase, awaiting assignments from the leader\\n4. STABLE - All members have joined and synced, group is operational\\n5. DEAD - Group metadata is being removed\\n\\nThe valid state transitions are enforced through the `validPreviousStates` set in `ClassicGroupState`, defining the valid transitions:\\n- EMPTY → PREPARING_REBALANCE\\n- PREPARING_REBALANCE → COMPLETING_REBALANCE or EMPTY\\n- COMPLETING_REBALANCE → STABLE\\n- STABLE/PREPARING_REBALANCE/COMPLETING_REBALANCE/EMPTY → DEAD\\n\\n**Join Phase Implementation:**\\nMember join state is tracked in `ClassicGroupMember.java` with methods `isAwaitingJoin()` which checks if `awaitingJoinFuture` is set. When members send join requests, the `classicGroupJoin()` method in `GroupMetadataManager.java` processes them and manages the group's transition to PREPARING_REBALANCE. The flow calls `addMemberThenRebalanceOrCompleteJoin()` and `maybePrepareRebalanceOrCompleteJoin()` to coordinate the state transitions.\\n\\n**Sync Phase Implementation:**\\nMember sync state is tracked with `isAwaitingSync()` checking if `awaitingSyncFuture` is set. The `classicGroupSync()` method in `GroupMetadataManager.java` handles sync requests from members. Once all members have synced with their assignments, the group transitions from COMPLETING_REBALANCE to STABLE.\\n\\n**State Transitions:**\\nState transitions are managed through the `transitionTo()` method in `ClassicGroup.java`, which enforces valid transitions and tracks both current and previous states. Invalid transitions throw an `IllegalStateException`.\\n\\n**Modern Groups:**\\nModern consumer groups (`ConsumerGroup.java` in modern/consumer/) implement their own state machine with states: EMPTY, ASSIGNING, RECONCILING, STABLE, DEAD.
